 yunaan or rome main to ghar-ghar main jupiter kii puja hoti thi
 But the Persian invaders broke down almost all the deities and temples of Athens city, the capital of Greece
 itnaa hi nahin, itnaa hi nahin, unhone athens nivaasiyon ko talwaar ke ghat utaar diya
 Even today the land beneath the ruins of these destroyed-corrupt sacred Dev temples is found to be ashed
 in yudhon ke samaapt hone par athens-nivaasiyon ne apni sari shakti lagaakar phir se apane dev-mandiron ko bananaa prarambh kiya
 The rulers of Athens were instrumental in the construction of these temples by the Pariklies, Artisans Collectinis and Sangatras Phidias
 in mahapurushon ke prayaas se ye dev-mandir itane sundar bane ki aaj tak sansar main inaki jod kaa koi bhi bhawan nahin ban sakaa
 Even today, the Athens dev-temples are considered to be the best buildings in the world, but these buildings remained dev temples for 1000 years
 iske baad 1000 varsh tak isaayiyon ke girjaghar or phir turk logon kii masjiden baniin or ab to ye sansar ke sabase bade khandhiron ke rup main sunsaan pade hai
 Skilled craftsmen and saints come from every corner of the world to study the work of Phidias by these deities 
 fedias kaa naam isa ke janm se lagbhag 464 varsh pehle prasiddh hona aarambh hua
 The ruler of Athens was his close friend and he entrusted Phidias to build all the Athens' deities, temples and monuments
 fedias saadhaaran manushya na tha
 He was the famous emperor of ancient times
 yah vilakshan vyakti keval apane aujaaron kaa prayog karne kii hi purna yogyata na rakhata tha, use un vishyon kaa bhi purna gyaan tha, jinka uske vyavsaay se sabandh tha, jaise itihaas, kavita, kalpit kahaniyaan, rekha-ganit, prakaash-vigyaan aadi
 First of all, Phidias taught the Greeks to imitate nature completely
 yunaan nivasee is anupam kalakaar ke kaaryo or paraamarsh kaa bada sammaan karte the
 He built a very exquisite statue of Minerva Devi
 hathi-daant or sone kii bani yah murti 39 foot oonchi he
 In this statue, Phidias also dug his own and his friend Pariklij's picture on the goddess's shield, and this is why the residents of Athens began to envy him
 at: unhone fedias par yah doshaaropan kiya ki usne devi kii murti ke saamaan kaa apharan kiya he
 Phidias, saddened by this bad behavior of the Athens-inhabitants, went to Olympia
 vahaan jaakar usne olympia ke jupiter devtaa kii us murti kaa nirmaan kiya
 It was a unique work of art and was counted among the seven wonders of the world
 yah murti hathi-daant or swarna se 30 foot oonchi banaai gai thi or iske prayek bhaag kaa anupaat purnataya thik tha
 Its splendor was also similar to the splendor of the temple
 iske saundarya ne yunaan desh ke dharm ko kahin adhik saundaryapurna bana diya tha
 That statue was the masterpiece of Phidias, and because of this statue, the name of Phidias and the country of Greece became forever immortal in the history of the world
 aise mahaan tyaagi or vidwaan kalakaar par uske deshavaasiyon ne duusari baar yah dosha lagaaya ki fedias ne apana tathaa apane mitra periclij kaa chitra devi kii murti kii dhaal par khodakar ghor adharm kiya he
